Laboratory Information: The descriptive (1) or (2), which appears after the day of some Faculty of Engineering and Computer Science course listings, indicates that the lab section is given on the day indicated and every 1st and alternate week of the term or every 2nd and alternate week of the term. Alternate week Laboratory Schedule: Fall Term: Week (1) labs start Monday, September 9, 2013. Week (2) labs start on Monday, September 16, 2013. Winter term: Week (1) labs start Monday, January 6, 2014. Week (2) labs start Monday, January 13, 2014.<br></td>
